<li>{@link #BOOTSTRAP_SERVERS_CONFIG \"bootstrap.servers\"}</li>\n139:  * </ul>\n140:  *\n141:  * By default, Kafka Streams does not allow users to overwrite the following properties (Streams setting ID</li>\n144:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#ENABLE_AUTO_COMMIT_CONFIG \"enable.auto.commit\"} (false) - Streams client will always disable/turn off auto committing</li>\n145:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#PARTITION_ASSIGNMENT_STRATEGY_CONFIG \"partition.assignment.strategy\"} (<code>StreamsPartitionAssignor</code>) - Streams client will always use its own partition assignor</li>\n146:  * </ul>\n147:  *\n148:  * If {@link #PROCESSING_GUARANTEE_CONFIG \"processing.guarantee\"} is set to {@link #EXACTLY_ONCE_V2 \"exactly_once_v2\"},\n149:  * Kafka Streams does not allow users to overwrite the following properties (Streams setting shown in parentheses):\n150:  * <ul>\n151:  *   <li>{@link ConsumerConfig#ISOLATION_LEVEL_CONFIG \"isolation.level\"} (read_committed) - Consumers will always read committed data only</li>\n152:  *   <li>{@link ProducerConfig#ENABLE_IDEMPOTENCE_CONFIG \"enable.idempotence\"} (true) - Producer will always have idempotency enabled</li>\n153:  * </ul>\n154:  *\n155:  * @see KafkaStreams#KafkaStreams(org.apache.kafka.streams.Topology, Properties)\n156:  * @see ConsumerConfig\n157:  * @see ProducerConfig\n158:  */\n159: public class
